Shanghai Local Court 213

Civil Judgments: Yang Yaoting vs. Chen Runmin et al. for Rent and Water Fees (Judgment): Defendant Chen Runmin shall pay the plaintiff's arrears of 290 taels of silver for rent and 10 yuan in silver dollars for water fees. Feng Yan shall pay the plaintiff's arrears of 180 yuan in silver dollars for rent and 10 yuan in silver dollars for street sweeping and water fees. Xue Peizhao shall pay the plaintiff's arrears of 180 yuan in silver dollars for rent and 10 yuan in silver dollars for street sweeping and water fees. Wan Rice Shop and Lu Ruitang shall pay the plaintiff's arrears of 496 yuan in silver dollars for rent and 20 yuan in silver dollars for street sweeping and water fees. Five Friends Store and Cen Qiwu shall pay the plaintiff's arrears of 280 yuan in silver dollars for rent and 10 yuan in silver dollars for street sweeping and water fees. The remainder of the plaintiff's claims are dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear two-tenths of the litigation costs, and the remaining costs shall be borne proportionally by each defendant. ▲ Xu Runsheng vs. Xiang Shunjin for Loan (Judgment): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 617 yuan and 9 jiao in silver dollars. Litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Zhu Wenbin vs. Zhu Yaozong for Membership Appeal (Judgment): The original judgment is overturned, and the appellee's lawsuit in the first instance is dismissed. The litigation costs of both instances shall be borne by the appellee. ▲ vs. for Rice Money Appeal (Judgment): The appeal is dismissed. The litigation costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant. ▲ Gui Fang vs. Zhou Yizhong for Loan (Judgment): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's loan of 800 yuan in silver dollars, plus interest at a rate of 5% per annum from July 1, 1930, until the date of execution. The remainder of the plaintiff's claims are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Du Baoyu vs. Ding Fanglin et al. for Rice Money (Judgment): Defendant Ding Fanglin shall pay the plaintiff's rice money of 68 yuan and 9 jiao in silver dollars. If unable to pay, Defendant Wu Dalun shall be responsible for paying on their behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by Defendant Ding Fanglin. ▲ Wu Ge vs. Cao Maosen for Goods Money (Judgment): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's goods money of 145 yuan in silver dollars. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Wu Zhongyang vs. Shao Baihua et al. for Rent Arrears (Judgment): Defendant Shao Baihua shall pay the plaintiff 128 yuan in silver dollars for rent, plus 32 jiao in small silver dollars. Zhang Shu shall pay the plaintiff 66 yuan and 6 jiao in silver dollars for rent, plus 36 jiao in small silver dollars. Fan Lianfa shall pay the plaintiff 118 yuan and 5 jiao in silver dollars for rent, plus 22 jiao in small silver dollars. He Chunyu shall pay the plaintiff 149 yuan and 5 jiao in silver dollars for rent, plus 22 jiao in small silver dollars, and shall all vacate the premises. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendants proportionally. ▲ Ding Bohua vs. He Xingyun for Rent Arrears (Judgment): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff's rent of 84 yuan in silver dollars. The plaintiff's claim for eviction is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant, except for the portion withdrawn and dismissed, which shall be borne by the plaintiff. ▲ Zhang Shunjie et al. vs. Gu Jingqing for Rent and Other Appeals (Judgment): The appeal is dismissed. The litigation costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant. ▲ Wei Xuru vs. Lin Baoying for Boundary Appeal (Judgment): The appeal is dismissed. The litigation costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant. Ying Zhou Shi vs. Ying Xinfu for Living Expenses (Judgment): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 22 yuan per month for household living expenses. The remainder of the plaintiff's claims are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by both parties individually. ▲ Jiang Hanqing vs. Sheng Shi for Bill Money (Judgment): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff's bill money of 1200 taels of silver. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Cao A Gen vs. Cao Yuansheng for Loan Appeal (Judgment): The appeal is dismissed. The litigation costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant. ▲ Ruling Sheng Ronggen vs. Fang Dajun for Compensation (Judgment): The lawsuit is rejected. The litigation costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant. ▲ Ye Feidiao vs. Ju Shilin for Mutual Lawsuits for Damages Appeal (Judgment): Both the appeal and the incidental appeal are dismissed. The litigation costs of the second instance shall be borne by both parties individually. ▲ Central Trust Company vs. Sun Yide et al. for Rent (Judgment): Defendant Sun Yide shall pay the plaintiff's rent of 5918 yuan and 3 jiao in silver dollars in six installments within one year from the date of the judgment (i.e., one installment every two months), plus interest at a rate of 5% per annum for each installment from May 1 of this year until the date of execution. If Sun Yide is unable to pay, Defendant Ye Pinhou shall be responsible for paying on their behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by Sun Yide. ▲ Shunchang Wool Store vs. Cao Xiji for Loan (Judgment): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's loan principal and interest totaling 11209 taels, 1 mace, and 1 fen of silver. The plaintiff's request for provisional execution is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant, except for the costs of the plaintiff's request for provisional execution, which shall be borne by the plaintiff. ▲ Chen Wu Shi vs. Shi Jielin for Loan (Judgment): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 100 yuan in silver dollars. Litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Zhao Yuting vs. Feng Guangda et al. for Rent Arrears (Judgment): Defendant Feng Guangda shall pay the plaintiff's rent of 24 yuan in silver dollars. Meng Helou shall pay the plaintiff's rent of 36 yuan in silver dollars. Li Baolan shall pay the plaintiff's rent of 80 yuan in silver dollars. Zhou Hanqing shall pay the plaintiff's rent of 40 yuan in silver dollars, and shall all vacate the premises. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendants proportionally.

Civil Execution Instructions: Wang Changsheng requests detention. According to the petition, come to the court for questioning at 2 pm on October 22nd. This instruction is issued. Shen Mingwen petitions for suspension of execution. According to the petition, this instruction is issued. ▲ Xiang Guisheng petitions for money. According to the petition, bring the certificate to the court for collection at 9 am on October 28th. This instruction is issued. ▲ Mei Shouchi petitions for execution. According to the petition, the debtor Cao Tianran has filed a lawsuit for payment against Fuxing et al. Proceed after the judgment in that case is finalized. The so-called execution against Liang Qitang is temporarily delayed. This instruction is issued. ▲ Wang Ding Shi et al. petition for suspension of execution. According to the petition, come to the court in person for questioning and verification. This instruction is issued. ▲ Jiang Fangzhou petitions for the release of the debtor. According to the petition, permission is granted for release. This instruction is issued. ▲ Wu Zilong petitions for case cancellation. According to the petition, permission is granted for case cancellation. This instruction is issued. ▲ Zhu Tingfang, for the Qiu Zuoyin goods money case, requests payment of custody and other fees. According to the petition, come to the court at 1 pm on the 21st of this month to clarify, verify, and issue payment. This instruction is issued. ▲ Wang Zhisui, for the Wang Weiqing loan case, requests compulsory execution. According to the petition, the debtor has been strictly limited to pay the money into the court by the 25th of this month. If the money is not paid by the deadline, please allow compulsory execution. This instruction is issued. ▲ Chu Yunqing, for the Ye Zhilin rent arrears case, requests the dispatch of personnel to enforce eviction. According to the petition, permission is granted to dispatch personnel to order eviction. This instruction is issued. ▲ Xu Zhifen, for the Yin Shunlin et al. mortgage money case, petitions for execution. According to the petition, wait for the case to be summoned for questioning. This instruction is issued. ▲ Jiang Zhaoqing petitions for execution. According to the petition, wait for the case to be summoned for questioning. This instruction is issued. ▲ Yang Xiuqing et al., regarding the auction of Zhou Zhikun's real estate, have rights and interests and petition for joint handling. According to the petition, wait for the judgment on the case in which the people sue Zhou Zhikun for money, and then come to file a statement to merge the case for review. This instruction is issued. ▲ Dao Shuangdasheng, for the Sha Shangzhen et al. debt case, continues to petition for execution. According to the petition, wait for the case to be summoned for questioning. This instruction is issued. ▲ Jia Chengzhang petitions for seizure. According to the petition, the debtor still owes 20 yuan in silver dollars, which has been continuously summoned for payment. The requested seizure of movable property is temporarily delayed. This instruction is issued. ▲ Shen Xingzheng petitions for ordering the objector to formally file a lawsuit and, after the deadline, exempting them from providing a guarantee to receive the case money. According to the petition, wait for review. This instruction is issued. ▲ Liu Hanqing petitions for case cancellation. According to the petition, permission is granted for case cancellation. This instruction is issued. ▲ Xu Juqing petitions for execution. According to the petition, the debtor has successively paid 249 yuan in silver dollars, leaving 83 yuan still owed. A deadline is set for full payment by the end of this month. Please be informed. This instruction is issued. ▲ Wang Shaolan petitions for execution. According to the petition, wait for the officer to handle it. This instruction is issued.

Instructions: Hu Wang Shi requests to retain the right to sue. According to the petition, if your daughter is injured by being beaten by her son-in-law, she should report the case and have an examination according to law. The request to retain the right to sue is not in accordance with the law and cannot be approved. This instruction is issued. ▲ Zhang Shunsong petitions for receiving a pension. According to the petition, you and others stated in court that you were unwilling to receive the Jianghai Customs pension. The request should not be discussed. This instruction is issued. ▲ Cai Xiaowei sues Gu Xianglin for enticing away his wife and requests to withdraw the complaint. According to the petition, the withdrawal of the complaint should be approved. This instruction is issued. ▲ Zhu Fengshan sues Peng Baolin for assault and requests to withdraw the complaint. According to the petition, the withdrawal of the complaint should be approved. This instruction is issued. ▲ Yang Linjiang sues Fan Xianying for fraud and requests exemption from prosecution. According to the petition, the case concerns a minor primary case with minor circumstances. Since the plaintiff does not wish to punish the defendant with a fine, the request for exemption from prosecution should be approved. This instruction is issued. ▲ Qiu Jinkuan sues Qiu Yuan Shi for theft. According to the petition, this case has been sent for delivery of the disposition order. ▲ Yang Rixiang petitions for instructions on the expiration date of the sentence of Yang Ji Shi et al. According to the petition, the sentence of Yang Ji Shi et al. will expire on November 30 of this year. Please be informed. This instruction is issued. (Above date is October 17th)
